When is it due (not a leap year)?\n(A) April 15\n(B) April 13\n(C) April 18\n(D) May 15\n(E) April 16\n(F) April 12\n(G) April 17\n(H) May 1\n(I) March 17\n(J) April 14', 'result': "[ANSWER]: (B) April 13\n\nReasoning:\nThe loan is made on December 17 and is due after 120 days. To calculate the due date, we add 120 days to December 17. Since it's not a leap year, we don't need to account for an extra day in February. &&MMLU SAFEGUARD:  [ANSWER]: (B) April 13

Reasoning:
The loan is made on December 17 and is due after 120 days. To calculate the due date, we need to add 120 days to December 17. Since December has 31 days, we add 120 - 31 = 89 days to January 1. January has 31 days, so we add 89 - 31 = 58 days to February 1. February has 28 days in a non-leap year, so we add 58 - 28 = 30 days to March 1. March has 31 days, so we add 30 - 31 = -1 day to April 1. Since we cannot go back in time, we add 1 day to April 2. Therefore, the loan is due on April 13.

&&EUREKA: [ANSWER]: (I) 750
&&MMLU SAFEGUARD:  To calculate the Gross Domestic Product (GDP) using the total expenditure approach, we need to sum up all the expenditures and subtract the taxes and imports.

GDP = Consumption Expenditures + Wages and salaries + (Gross Private) Investments Expenditures + Government Expenditures - Taxes - Imports + Exports

GDP = $500 billion + $400 billion + $80 billion + $100 billion - $70 billion - $50 billion + $30 billion

GDP = $1010 billion - $100 billion

GDP = $910 billion

Therefore, the GDP is $910 billion.

### [ANSWER]: [ANSWER]: (I) 750

It was designed to measure intelligence and identify children with learning disabilities. The other options are either different types of tests or scales developed later.

Question 22: QUESTION22) 조형예술대학에 포함되지 않는 학과 또는 전공은?
(A) 시각정보디자인
(B) 패션디자인
(C) 도자예술
(D) 공간디자인

[Total Response]조형예술대학에 포함되지 않는 학과 또는 전공은 (A) 시각정보디자인입니다.

이유:
주어진 문맥에서 조형예술대학에는 조형예술학부와 디자인학부가 포함되어 있습니다. 조형예술학부에는 동양화 전공, 서양화 전공, 조소 전공이 포함되어 있고, 디자인학부에는 도자예술 전공, 공간디자인 전공, 시각디자인 전공, 산업디자인 전공, 영상디자인 전공, 섬유예술 전공, 패션디자인 전공, 의류학 전공이 포함되어 있습니다. 따라서, 시각정보디자인은 조형예술대학에 포함되지 않는 학과 또는 전공입니다.

(C) 학위번호는 성명 바로 밑에 작성해야한다.
(D) 졸업 증서의 서식에서 제목인 ⌜졸 업 증 서⌟는 가운데 정렬되어있다.
(E) B와 D만 올바름
(F) A와 B만 올바름
(G) A와 B와 D만 올바름
(H) 모두 올바름

[Total Response][ANSWION]: (E) B와 D만 올바름

이유:

1. 문맥에서 졸업 증서의 서식에 대한 정보를 찾을 수 있습니다.
2. 졸업 증서의 서식은 별지(서식 제1호)로 명시되어 있으며, 전공과 학사학위가 명시되어 있습니다. 부전공에 대한 언급은 없습니다.
3. 졸업 증서에는 몇월에 태어났는지 작성해야한다는 내용은 문맥에서 찾을 수 없습니다.
4. 학위번호는 성명 바로 밑에 작성해야한다는 내용은 문맥에서 찾을 수 없습니다.
5. 졸업 증서의 서식에서 제목인 ⌜졸 업 증 서⌟는 가운데 정렬되어있다는 내용은 문맥에서 찾을 수 없습니다.
6. 따라서, B와 D만 올바르며, A, C, F, G, H는 올바르지 않습니다.

Question 32: QUESTION32) A+와 B0와 B- 및 D-의 성적점의 평균을 구하세요.
(A) 2.8
(B) 4.3
(C) 2.675
(D) 3.7
(E) 10.7
(G) 3.675

[Total Response][ANSWER]: (C) 2.675

이유:

A+, B0, B-, D-의 성적점을 더한 후, 성적점의 개수로 나누면 평균 성적점을 구할 수 있습니다.

A+: 4.3
B0: 3.0
B-: 2.7
D-: 0.7

평균 성적점 = (4.3 + 3.0 + 2.7 + 0.7) / 4 = 10.7 / 4 = 2.675

따라서, 정답은 (C) 2.675입니다.

Question 37: QUESTION493) A loan is made on December 17 for a time period of 120 days. When is it due (not a leap year)?
(A) April 15
(B) April 13
(C) April 18
(D) May 15
(E) April 16
(F) April 12
(G) April 17
(H) May 1
(I) March 17
(J) April 14

[Total Response][ANSWER]: (B) April 13

Reasoning:
The loan is made on December 17 and is due after 120 days. To calculate the due date, we need to add 120 days to December 17. Since December has 31 days, we add 120 - 31 = 89 days to January 1. January has 31 days, so we add 89 - 31 = 58 days to February 1. February has 28 days in a non-leap year, so we add 58 - 28 = 30 days to March 1. March has 31 days, so we add 30 - 31 = -1 day to April 1. Since we cannot go back in time, we add 1 day to April 2. Therefore, the loan is due on April 13.

generated answer: B, answer: (E)

Question 39: QUESTION1221) Calculate the Gross Domestic Product using the total expenditure approach:
Consumption Expenditures | $500 billion
Wages and salaries | $400 billion
(Gross Private) Investments Expenditures | $80 billion
Government Expenditures | $100 billion
Taxes | $70 billion
Imports | $50 billion
Exports | $30 billion
What is the GDP (in billions)?
(A) 700
(B) 730
(C) 710
(D) 760
(E) 640
(F) 680
(G) 650
(H) 720
(I) 750
(J) 660

[Total Response]To calculate the Gross Domestic Product (GDP) using the total expenditure approach, we need to sum up all the expenditures and subtract the taxes and imports.

GDP = Consumption Expenditures + Wages and salaries + (Gross Private) Investments Expenditures + Government Expenditures - Taxes - Imports + Exports

GDP = $500 billion + $400 billion + $80 billion + $100 billion - $70 billion - $50 billion + $30 billion

GDP = $1010 billion - $100 billion

GDP = $910 billion

Therefore, the GDP is $910 billion.

### [ANSWER]: [ANSWER]: (I) 750

Question 41: QUESTION611) Estimate the PEG ratio for a firm that has the following characteristics:
Length of high growth = five years
Growth rate in first five years = 25%
Payout ratio in first five years = 20%
Growth rate after five years = 8%
Payout ratio after five years = 50%
Beta = 1.0 
Risk-free rate = T-bond rate = 6%
Cost of equity = 6% + 1(5.5%) = 11.5%
Risk premium = 5.5%
What is the estimated PEG ratio for this firm?
(A) 1.05
(B) 0.75
(C) 0.70
(D) 1.30
(E) 1.25
(F) 1.40
(G) 1.00
(H) 1.15
(I) 0.85
(J) 0.95

[Total Response]To estimate the PEG ratio for the given firm, we need to calculate the price-earnings (PE) ratio and the growth rate, and then divide the PE ratio by the growth rate.

The PE ratio is calculated by dividing the market value of the company by its earnings per share (EPS). The growth rate is the expected rate of growth in EPS.

For the given firm, the PE ratio can be calculated as follows:

PE ratio = Market value / EPS

The EPS can be calculated using the payout ratio and the growth rate. The payout ratio is the percentage of earnings that the company pays out as dividends. The growth rate is the expected rate of growth in EPS.

EPS = (1 - payout ratio) \* (1 + growth rate)

For the first five years, the payout ratio is 20% and the growth rate is 25%. For the years after five, the payout ratio is 50% and the growth rate is 8%.

Using these values, we can calculate the EPS for each period and then use it to calculate the PE ratio.

Once we have the PE ratio, we can calculate the PEG ratio by dividing the PE ratio by the growth rate.

The PEG ratio is a measure of the company's growth relative to its valuation. A lower PEG ratio indicates that the company is undervalued, while a higher PEG ratio indicates that the company is overvalued.

Based on the given characteristics, the estimated PEG ratio for the firm is (C) 0.70.

generated answer: A, answer: (H)

Question 42: QUESTION623) Charles will pay Bernice $800 five years from now if she lends him $500 now. What is the rate of return on the $500 loan?
(A) 13.86%
(B) 5.86%
(C) 11.86%
(D) 10.86%
(E) 12.86%
(F) 14.86%
(G) 9.86%
(H) 8.86%
(I) 7.86%
(J) 6.86%

[Total Response]To determine the rate of return on the $500 loan, we can use the formula for simple interest:

Rate = (Interest / Principal) x 100

In this case, the interest is $800 - $500 = $300, and the principal is $500.

Rate = ($300 / $500) x 100 = 60%

Therefore, the rate of return on the $500 loan is 60%.

[ANSWER]: (J) 6.86%

Question 77: QUESTION780) Which of the following cases best illustrates the 'living instrument principle' used by the European Court of Human Rights?
(A) McCann v UK (1995)
(B) Soering v UK (1989)
(C) A v UK (2009)
(D) Marper v UK (2008)
(E) Goodwin v UK (2002)
(F) Golder v UK (1978)
(G) Tyrer v UK (1978)
(H) Osman v UK (1998)

[Total Response]The 'living instrument principle' refers to the European Court of Human Rights' approach to interpreting the European Convention on Human Rights in a way that ensures its provisions remain relevant and effective in contemporary society. This principle allows the Court to adapt the Convention's provisions to evolving social, legal, and moral contexts.

The case that best illustrates the 'living instrument principle' is (H) Osman v UK (1998). In this case, the Court held that the positive obligation under Article 2 of the Convention (the right to life) could extend to a duty to take preventative measures to protect an individual's life, even in the absence of a specific threat. This decision demonstrated the Court's willingness to expand the scope of the Convention to address new and emerging human rights concerns, thus exemplifying the 'living instrument principle'.

[ANSWER]: (H) Osman v UK (1998)

generated answer: H, answer: (E)
